Cocoon Cleaning Summary


1. Table Summary


The table is about Facebook ad creative details. It contains information like ad IDs, account IDs, page links, UTM parameters, ad descriptions, and image hashes. The data includes details for ad creatives such as link data, captions, call-to-action buttons, and app specifications. Each row represents a unique ad creative with its associated metadata and tracking information.
